# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags unthreaded double -lm -lrt -O0  ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded double -lm -lrt -O0 ; \
   rm temp.txt

   rm temp.txt

# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags unthreaded __fp16 -lm -lrt -O0  ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded __fp16 -lm -lrt -O0 ; \
   rm temp.txt

# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags unthreaded double -lm -lrt -O0 -funroll-loops ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded double -lm -lrt -O0 -funroll-loops; \
   rm temp.txt

           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values 2 threads double -lm -lrt -O0 -funroll-loops; \
   rm temp.txt

# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning_threaded multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags 2 threads double -lm -lrt -O1  ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values 2 threads double -lm -lrt -O1 ; \
   rm temp.txt

       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded double -lm -lrt -O2 -funroll-loops; \
   rm temp.txt

# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags unthreaded float -lm -lrt -Ofast  ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded float -lm -lrt -Ofast ; \
   rm temp.txt

# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning_threaded multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags 16 threads __fp16 -lm -lrt -Ofast -funroll-loops ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values 16 threads __fp16 -lm -lrt -Ofast -funroll-loops; \
   rm temp.txt

# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags unthreaded double -lm -lrt -Os  ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded double -lm -lrt -Os ; \
   rm temp.txt

counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags 4 threads float -lm -lrt -Os -funroll-loops ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values 4 threads float -lm -lrt -Os -funroll-loops; \
   rm temp.txt

g++  -ITools -lm -lrt -Og  -c Tools/Timer.cpp -o obj/Timer.o
g++  -o bin/CHeterodyning obj/CHeterodyning.o obj/Timer.o -lm -lrt -Og 
# a simple shell script to run CHeterodyning multiple times, writting the flags and then the values on the same line of a csv file on the root (..) folder
counter=10  ; \
   cd .. && python3 write_flags.py flags unthreaded double -lm -lrt -Og  ; \
   while [ $counter -gt 0 ]; \
       do \
           C/bin/CHeterodyning; \
           counter=$(( $counter - 1)); \
       done; \
   python3 write_flags.py values unthreaded double -lm -lrt -Og ; \
   rm temp.txt
